    <p class="attributed-text-segment-list__content text-color-text !text-sm whitespace-pre-wrap break-words
        " dir="ltr" data-test-id="main-feed-activity-card__commentary">🍻📄 Behind every great festival — and every great business — is masterful organization.

With the world’s largest festival, Oktoberfest, in full swing, we see striking parallels between this logistical marvel and Lexmark's document solutions. Oktoberfest organizers coordinate:

👨👩👧👦 Millions of visitors across multiple venues
🥨 Seamless supply chains for hundreds of vendors
♻️ Efficient waste management systems

Similarly, Lexmark systems orchestrate:
🔄 Your enterprise's document ecosystem
🔒 Secure information flow to the right people
📊 Resource optimization with minimal waste

And for our Lexmark Germany/DACH team’s cherished tradition of hosting clients and partners at the “Lexmark Wiesn”, we have our master coordinators <a class="link" href="https://de.linkedin.com/in/olaf-tusche-90a898201?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>Olaf Tusche</a> and <a class="link" href="https://de.linkedin.com/in/stefanie-tusche-257b627b?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>Stefanie Tusche</a> who go above and beyond in organizing our two events every year and masterfully handling complexity behind the scenes to make sure our guests have a good time, and the Bavarian sky always stays white and blue 🌤️🩵

A big shoutout to Olaf and Stefanie and a huge “Thank you” to all of our clients and partners for attending another great “Lemark Wiesn” with us!

<a class="link" href="https://uk.linkedin.com/in/dannymolhoek?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>Danny Molhoek</a> <a class="link" href="https://de.linkedin.com/in/michael-lang-3b30257?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>Michael Lang</a></p>

Xerox and Lexmark solutions provide:  
📊 Intelligent data capture to inform business decisions

        " dir="ltr" data-test-id="main-feed-activity-card__commentary">🦸♀️ The Unseen Heroes of the Office: Always ready when it matters most!

It's 4:58 p.m. The boardroom presentation is tomorrow at 8 a.m. The team just finalized the deck and needs 15 color copies. Who saves the day? Your reliable Lexmark printer, delivering flawless prints without drama.

Every day, Lexmark devices quietly power your success stories:

📊 That crucial contract, printed with perfect clarity seconds before the CEO walks in

📱 That last-minute design change, submitted remotely and printed instantly for the waiting client

These moments might seem small, but they're the difference between "We've got this" and "We have a problem."

From our expanded A4 portfolio to cutting-edge cloud services and enhanced security protocols, we're focused on creating solutions that make your hybrid workplace more efficient and secure.

The line between digital and physical documents continues to blur — and we're here for it. What print innovation would make your workday easier? Share below! ✨

    <a href="/uas/login?fromSignIn=true&amp;session_redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.linkedin.com%2Fcompany%2Flexmark&amp;trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card_ellipsis-menu-semaphore-sign-in-redirect&amp;guestReportContentType=POST&amp;_f=guest-reporting" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card_ellipsis-menu-semaphore-sign-in-redirect" data-tracking-will-navigate data-item-type="semaphore" data-semaphore-content-type="POST" data-semaphore-content-urn="urn:li:activity:7368588516877844480" data-semaphore-tracking-prefix="organization_guest_main-feed-card_ellipsis-menu-semaphore" data-is-logged-in="false" data-modal="semaphore__toggle" class="semaphore__toggle visited:text-color-text-secondary ellipsis-menu__semaphore ellipsis-menu__item-button flex items-center w-full p-1 cursor-pointer font-sans text-sm font-bold link-styled focus:link-styled link:no-underline active:bg-color-background-container-tint focus:bg-color-background-container-tint hover:bg-color-background-container-tint outline-offset-[-2px]" role="menuitem">

                      Bu yayını rapor et

  <div class="attributed-text-segment-list__container relative mt-1 mb-1.5 babybear:mt-0 babybear:mb-0.5">
    <p class="attributed-text-segment-list__content text-color-text !text-sm whitespace-pre-wrap break-words
        " dir="ltr" data-test-id="main-feed-activity-card__commentary">“The Digital Product Passport emphasises our circular economy commitment, meeting the needs of increasingly ESG-conscious buyers.”

<a class="link" href="https://be.linkedin.com/in/maxime-furkel-4114986?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>Maxime Furkel</a>, Director Government Relations, Lexmark EMEA participated in a panel discussion at <a class="link" href="https://be.linkedin.com/company/ce-rise-project?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>CE-RISE Project</a>’s annual conference in Geneva yesterday, outlining the opportunities and challenges in the implementation of Digital Product Passports for a global corporation.

According to Maxime, benefits of the Digital Product Passport (DPP) - a structured digital record that contains detailed information about a product’s lifecycle - are centered around four pillars:

1️⃣  User Information: Boosting confidence in remanufactured products and informed purchasing decisions
2️⃣  Product Traceability: Verified lifecycle data reinforcing credibility and sustainability marketing
3️⃣  End-of-Life Management: Speeding up End-of-Life (EoL) decisions, reducing shipments and minimizing the environmental impact
4️⃣  Compliance: Centralised digital DPP reducing labeling/packaging costs and enhancing operational efficiency

Among other things, the DPP’s upside potential lies in:
📊 Data transparency depending on consistent, high-quality input; there is a need for harmonised standards and infrastructure
🛂 While DPPs provide the data foundation, practical decisions still rely heavily on expert evaluation.
🏭 B2B vs. B2C differentiation is essential as the level of product history detail and disclosure needed for businesses differs from what end-consumers require.

“While we consider the need for harmonisation, EU-wide but also globally, as critical, we think that companies should be given the entrepreneurial flexibility and freedom to continue investing in their own EoL solutions. This will bring forward the best ideas to boost remanufacturing. With Lexmark now being part of <a class="link" href="https://www.linkedin.com/company/xerox?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>Xerox</a>, we will continue to drive innovative circular economy concepts – with even more scale, resources and expertise,” Maxime summarised.

Thank you to the entire CE-RISE team, especially <a class="link" href="https://no.linkedin.com/in/miguel-las-heras?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>Miguel Las Heras Hernández</a>, <a class="link" href="https://be.linkedin.com/in/magdalena-charytanowicz-pierard-4447098a?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>Magdalena Charytanowicz-Pierard</a> and <a class="link" href="https://no.linkedin.com/in/cristina-b-b-guerreiro-5a295432?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>Cristina B. B. Guerreiro</a>, for organising and hosting this important event and bringing together high-profile experts from around Europe united in their mission to push for circularity.♻️</p>
<!---->  </div>

        " dir="ltr" data-test-id="main-feed-activity-card__commentary">📚✏️ Pop quiz: What prints homework, syllabi, hall passes, and never needs a summer break? Answer: Lexmark printers!

As students and teachers head back to classrooms, educational institutions need print solutions that can keep pace with the academic year's demands. From day one orientation packets to final exam materials, Lexmark delivers reliability when it matters most.

Our solutions provide:

🔄 Versatile multifunction capabilities for copying, scanning, and printing

♻️ Eco-friendly options that teach sustainability by example

⚙️ Rugged reliability designed for high-volume, shared environments

🌎 Translation Assistant, which helps bridge the communication gaps in multicultural school communities

Whether you're outfitting a K-12 district or a university campus, our solutions can help design a print environment that makes the grade all year long.

Happy Back-to-School Season!</p>

    <p class="attributed-text-segment-list__content text-color-text !text-sm whitespace-pre-wrap break-words
        " dir="ltr" data-test-id="main-feed-activity-card__commentary">The Lexmark team in Cebu, Philippines, recently hosted a site visit from <a class="link" href="https://www.linkedin.com/company/xerox?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>Xerox</a> Chief Administrative Officer and Global Head of Operations Louie Pastor and Chief People Officer Kim Kleps.

Their visit reinforced strategic alignment, highlighted Cebu’s innovation and talent, and collaboration across teams.

“I'm extremely grateful to the Cebu team for their enthusiasm and openness in showcasing their capabilities and their sincere commitment to the success of our clients, partners and employees.” - 𝑳𝒐𝒖𝒊𝒆 𝑷𝒂𝒔𝒕𝒐𝒓

“It was a privilege to meet the team in Cebu, learn about their capabilities, and hear their perspectives on our Reinvention journey.” - 𝑲𝒊𝒎 𝑲𝒍𝒆𝒑𝒔

“This visit from Louie and Kim was more than symbolic; it was a powerful affirmation of Cebu’s strategic importance to Xerox.”  - 𝑺𝒕𝒆𝒑𝒉𝒂𝒏 𝑩𝒊𝒍𝒚, who leads Cebu operations</p>

📊 A powerful communication tool that captures attention in ways screens cannot

🎨 A canvas for vibrant, high-resolution images that bring your brand to life

📝 A tangible connection between your business and your customers

At Lexmark, we're not just about putting toner on paper—we're about transforming how your business communicates, connects, and convinces.

    <p class="attributed-text-segment-list__content text-color-text !text-sm whitespace-pre-wrap break-words
        attributed-text-segment-list__content-truncated" dir="ltr" data-test-id="main-feed-activity-card__commentary">When your tech goes down, it’s not just annoying—it’s expensive. Every minute of downtime is a minute you’re not getting things done (or making money). That’s why Lexmark is dialing things up in Australia with a smarter, faster, and downright better service model designed to keep your business humming. 
  
Lexmark’s newly enhanced service setup is all about turbocharging response times and beefing up reliability—especially for our friends in regional areas. What this means for you: Fewer headaches, quicker fixes, and more time to focus on what really matters: running your business like a boss. 

Backed by cutting-edge tech and a nationwide team of sharp-as-a-tack technicians, Lexmark boasts a first-time fix rate of over 90%. By fine-tuning service zones, Lexmark is aiming to offer 75% of Australians onsite or near-onsite service in under 48 hours. It’s just one more way we’re showing up (and showing off) our commitment to Aussie businesses. 
  
Curious about what this means for you? Roger Harvey, Lexmark's Service Manager for ANZ and Asia Pacific Central dives deeper into what customers can expect—and how Lexmark’s got your back. </p>

      Devam Et seçeneğini tıklayarak veya oturum açarak LinkedIn <a href="/legal/user-agreement?trk=linkedin-tc_auth-button_user-agreement" target="_blank" data-tracking-control-name="linkedin-tc_auth-button_user-agreement" data-tracking-will-navigate="true">Kullanıcı Anlaşması’nı</a>, <a href="/legal/privacy-policy?trk=linkedin-tc_auth-button_privacy-policy" target="_blank" data-tracking-control-name="linkedin-tc_auth-button_privacy-policy" data-tracking-will-navigate="true">Gizlilik Politikası’nı</a> ve <a href="/legal/cookie-policy?trk=linkedin-tc_auth-button_cookie-policy" target="_blank" data-tracking-control-name="linkedin-tc_auth-button_cookie-policy" data-tracking-will-navigate="true">Çerez Politikası’nı</a> kabul etmiş olursunuz.
